***нескромный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нескромный.html>нескро́мный</a> (23522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нескромный.html>нескро́мный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neskrómnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нескро́мнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нескро́мней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>immodest</li>
<li>indiscreet, indelicate</li>
<li>brazen</li></ol>

***несмотря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> (1001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesmotrjá na</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>in spite of, despite <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the action must be completed in advance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:серьезный.html>серьёзную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:наконец.html>наконе́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врачи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вылечить.html>вы́лечили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nesmotrjá na</b> serʹjóznuju boléznʹ, nakonéc vračí výlečili menjá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Despite</b> the bad illness, the doctors finally cured me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положительный.html>положи́тельную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:конференция.html>конфере́нция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закончиться.html>зако́нчилась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бедствие.html>бе́дствием</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nesmotrjá na</b> položítelʹnuju obstanóvku, konferéncija zakónčilasʹ bédstvijem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Despite</b> the positive atmosphere, the conference ended with a disaster.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>notwithstanding</li>
<li>although</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> underage <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of individuals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***несомненно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несомненно.html>несомне́нно</a> (3102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несомненный.html>несомне́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesomnénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несомненно.html>несомне́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesomnénno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>doubtlessly</li>
<li>undoubtedly, without doubt</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельный.html>несостоя́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesostojátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesostojátelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>insolvency, failure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объявить.html>объяви́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obʺjavítʹ o <b>nesostojátelʹnosti</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">declare bankruptcy</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>modest means</li>
<li>unfoundedness, groundlessness, flimsiness, unsoundness</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:состоятельный.html>состоя́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sostojátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельный.html>несостоя́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesostojátelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>insolvent</li>
<li>not wealthy, of modest means</li>
<li>unfounded, groundless, flimsy, unsound, untenable</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неспроста.html>неспроста́</a> (13937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">спроста́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sprostá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сравнить.html>сравни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sravnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ющийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнимый.html>сравни́мым</a> n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">В сущности, это практическая отработка стиля, постав пера, контакт слова и реальности, доводимый до автоматизма, ежедневная тренировка руки, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">несравнимая</span> по эффективности ни с какими «уроками чистописания», ― вот это добровольное дневниковое тягло. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

***нестерпимо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимо.html>нестерпи́мо</a> (9336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesterpímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимо.html>нестерпи́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesterpímo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unbearably
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “хори́стка  | The Chorus Girl | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> |  republished in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Русский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></cite>, 2002:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимо.html>нестерпи́мо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жаркий.html>жа́рко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душный.html>ду́шно</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Býlo <b>nesterpímo</b> žárko i dúšno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It was <b>unbearably</b> hot and stifling.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимо.html>нестерпи́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesterpímo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesterpímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
